andira: (6) small genus of evergreen trees of tropical America and western Africa
anuran: (6) any of various tailless stout-bodied amphibians with long hind limbs for leaping; semiaquatic and terrestrial species
callus: (6) an area of skin that is thick or hard from continual pressure or friction (as the sole of the foot)
gilder: (6) someone whose occupation is to apply an overlay of gold or gilt
irani : (5) a native or inhabitant of Iran
lienal: (6) of or relating to the spleen
nolina: (6) perennial plants resembling yucca; found in southern United States and Mexico
orion : (5) (Greek mythology) a giant Boeotian hunter who pursued the Pleiades and was eventually slain by Artemis; was then placed in the sky as a constellation
rant  : (4) a loud bombastic declamation expressed with strong emotion
salt  : (4) a compound formed by replacing hydrogen in an acid by a metal (or a radical that acts like a metal)
vigna : (5) genus of vines or erect herbs having trifoliate leaves and yellowish or purplish flowers; of warm or tropical regions; most species often placed in genus Phaseolus
vocal : (5) music intended to be performed by one or more singers, usually with instrumental accompaniment
